A query string is parsed by the `Parser` class into an AST.\\n2. The AST is passed to the `Optimizer` which generates an optimized `ExecutionPlan`.\\n3. The `ExecutionEngine` is instantiated from the optimized plan.\\n4. The engine creates a tree of `ExecutionBlock` objects based on execution nodes.\\n5. During execution, blocks interact with `RocksDBCollection` to retrieve data from storage.\\n6. The `TransactionState` ensures ACID properties for all data operations.\\n7. The `Methods` class provides the transaction API that coordinates all operations.\\n\\nThis architecture demonstrates a clean separation of concerns: parsing handles syntax, optimization handles planning, the execution engine handles coordination, blocks handle specific operations, the collection interface handles storage access, and the transaction system ensures consistency.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
